Use your eraser button on the pen to remove both ink strokes and existing notation. You can also draw freehand on the score, using the sketch layer, to quickly brainstorm and leave notes/comments for yourself and others.\r\n\r\nPRINT YOUR RESULTS\r\nStaffPad will intelligently layout the score when it’s time to print.
